<userid>116312585587757918302</userid><Text>Update: start the trail in reverse. One side of the trail is more desert mountain terrain and the other has a ‚Äúhidden forest‚Äù vibe. There‚Äôs lots of high grass along the trail so be mindful of where you plant your feet. The trail is pretty decently maintained and there are lots of smaller trails that break off. You could easily spend an entire day just exploring.

Finally got to this location on a quiet day when there was relatively no one else around. Trail was difficult to navigate but I think that was on my map and inexperience not the location. The river near the bridge is beautiful. Not much shade so make sure you come prepared and I heard several rattles nearby so I‚Äôll be getting a snake bite kit before heading out again.</Text>< GmapID>

<user_name>Diana Lynn< /user_name><Date>1550205033970<//Date><Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
Best little Chinese restaurant in the county! $8.95 for a beautiful weekday lunch with entree, rice,  soup and wontons.  Our server was a lady named Lily and she took over the entire dining room from seating to fetching the drinks, taking orders, serving the food,  waiting on everyone's beckoning call for a little extra this and little extra that and "can I have a to go  Box." She even bussed all of the tables Single handedly.  Lily is a tiny little woman but she is so strong and can deliver about 5 plates at a time with a smile on her face! We never saw her sweat. Awesome service and awesome attitude.   We let her know it and we tipped her cash handsomely.  Lily is the most amazing wait staff we have ever experienced.  Unbelievable that she did this all on her own within the 90 minutes that we were there. There was a lady at the cash register but she was cold and just making out the bills and taking money. Did not help lift one finger for Lily. The food was absolutely amazing!  Today was our 1st experience there as we just recently moved to the neighborhood. We will definitely become regulars at this restaurant.</Review>

< review>
Came in here this past week for an early afternoon lunch. The location is great since its right in "downtown" Oxnard near the movie theater.

Some of the pros are that its not too expensive, the customer service is good and the food isn't too greasy (depending on what you get) like it is at a lot of other Chinese food places.

Some of the cons the food, for the most part, lacked flavor. I got a shrimp dish and that was really bland. The rice was okay though. The soup that the brought us at the beginning wasn't too appealing. I'm not too familiar with Chinese food but to me it looked like chicken fat mixed with egg and corn, not appealing.<//review>

Here‚Äôs my unsolicited advice to LTEC: Perhaps what you need is some really good coffee to go with your cakes ‚Äì good beans and a proper coffee counter. I bought their vegan S‚Äômores cupcake to go ($3.25). It turned out to be very good. Good texture, fresh, and with a decadent topping (which is what a cupcake is all about). Baked fresh, no preservatives, gluten-free also available (and gluten-free + vegan together). Recommended.
